"19";"Area of responsibility:
The role of Demi Chef works predominantly alone in the kitchen due to the size and nature of the room service operation.  You will be responsible for preparing room service orders from our hotel guests and members for breakfast, lunch and dinner.  You will also prepare staff food for the staff restaurant (50 employees).  The chef on duty is responsible for temperature checks, ordering, stock take and working closely with the Room Service team.  Chefs are required to be flexible and able to work early, late and weekend shifts.  Early shifts start at 6am until 2.30pm, and late shifts start at 2.30pm until 11pm.  Chefs work 5 days / 40 hours per week, we do not operate split shifts. We are looking for:
A qualified chef to join our small team in the room service department of 47 Park Street - Grand Residences by Marriott.  Experience in a fine dining kitchen is essential.  We are looking for a chef who is creative and looks for ways to improve operations.  As the chef will work alone you will be required to have confidence, initiative and excellent communication skills to hand over information to the rest of the team.  As we are a high standard luxury hotel we require a high standard of grooming and a good command of English.  Applicants must be eligible to work in the UK (German / EU candidates are eligible to work)."
